1b1(sna tshogs): rgya gar skad du/ Ar+ya su bi krAn ta bi krA mi pa ri pr-its+tsha pradz+nyA pA ra mi tA
1b2(sna tshogs): nir de sha/ bod skad du/ 'phags pa rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pas zhus
1b3(sna tshogs): pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bstan pa// // bam po dang po/
2a1(sna tshogs): sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' dang / 'phags pa nyan thos thams
2a2(sna tshogs): cad la phyag 'tshal lo/ / 'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das rgyal
2a3(sna tshogs): po'i khab na/ 'od ma'i tshal bya ka lan ta ka gnas pa na/ dge slong stong nyis brgya lnga bcu'i
2a4(sna tshogs): dge slong gi dge 'dun chen po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po/ sangs rgyas
2b1(sna tshogs): kyi zhing tha dad pa nas 'dus pa/ skye ba gcig gis thogs pa tshad med grangs med pa dang thabs cig tu bzhugs te//
2b2(sna tshogs): de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das 'khor brgya stong du mas yongs su bskor cing mdun gyis bltas te chos ston to//
2b3(sna tshogs): de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa zhes bya ba 'khor de nyid du 'dus
2b4(sna tshogs): par gyur nas 'dug pa de stan las langs te/ bla gos phrag pa gcig tu gzar nas/ pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa
2b5(sna tshogs): la btsugs te/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba de logs su thal mo sbar ba btud nas/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di
3a1(sna tshogs): skad ces gsol to/ / gal te zhus nas zhu ba lung bstan pa'i slad du/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bdag la
3a2(sna tshogs): skabs phye na/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas la bdag phyogs 'ga' zhig zhu lags so// /
3a3(sna tshogs): de skad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par
3a4(sna tshogs): gnon pa la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to/ / rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang
3a5(sna tshogs): dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas la khyod ci dang ci 'dod pa dris shig dang / dris pa de dang de'i lung bstan pas khyod kyi sems rangs
3a6(sna tshogs): par bya'o/ / de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang // bcom ldan 'das la/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po
3b1(sna tshogs): rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pas 'di skad ces gsol to/ / bcom ldan 'das shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bgyi ba/ bcom ldan
3b2(sna tshogs): 'das ji tsam gyis na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bgyi/ bcom ldan 'das ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' sems
3b3(sna tshogs): dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa lags/ bcom ldan 'das ji ltar na shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen
3b4(sna tshogs): po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ba lags/ bcom ldan 'das ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol
3b5(sna tshogs): tu phyin pa bsgom pa na/ bdud sdig can gyis glags mi rnyed cing / bdud kyi las thams cad kyang rtogs par 'gyur ba lags/ bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems
3b6(sna tshogs): dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas pa ji lta bus gnas na/ myur du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi chos yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ba lags/
3b7(sna tshogs): de skad ces gsol pa dang // bcom ldan 'das kyis/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa la 'di skad ces bka'
4a1(sna tshogs): sbal to/ / rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa khyod/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi don dang / ci nas khyod skye bo mang po la
4a2(sna tshogs): phan pa dang / skye bo mang po la bde ba dang / 'jig rten la snying brtse ba dang / lha dang mi rnams kyi skye bo phal po che'i don dang / phan pa dang / bde ba'i phyir zhus shing //
4a3(sna tshogs): da ltar gyi dang / ma 'ongs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams la snang ba byed par 'dod pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs
4a4(sna tshogs): pa'i sangs rgyas la/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'dri ba legs so legs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis mkhyen bzhin du/ byang chub sems dpa'
4a5(sna tshogs): sems dpa' chen po rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to/ / rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa khyod don gyi dbang gang mthong nas/ de
4a6(sna tshogs): bzhin gshegs pa la don 'di lta bu 'dri/ de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / bcom ldan 'das la/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rab kyi rtsal gyis
4a7(sna tshogs): rnam par gnon pas 'di skad ces gsol to/ / bcom ldan 'das sems can thams cad la sman pa dang / sems can thams cad la snying brtse ba dang / sems can
4b1(sna tshogs): thams cad kyi don gyi slad du/ bdag de bzhin gshegs pa la don 'di zhu lags so// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das/ 'di lta ste/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu
4b2(sna tshogs): phyin pa ni nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' dang / yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos dang / chos thams cad sdud pa lags pa'i
4b3(sna tshogs): slad du'o/ / bcom ldan 'das de la sems can gang dag nyan thos kyi theg pa la nges par gyur pa de dag gis thos na myur du zag pa ma mchis pa'i sa mngon sum du bgyid par 'gyur ba
4b4(sna tshogs): dang / gang dag rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la nges par gyur pa de dag kyang myur du rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pas nges par 'byung bar 'gyur ba dang / gang dag bla na med pa yang dag par
4b5(sna tshogs): rdzogs pa'i byang chub la yang dag par zhugs pa de dag kyang myur du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ba dang / gang dag yang dag
4b6(sna tshogs): pa nyid skyon med pa la ma zhugs shing sa gsum la ma nges pa de dag gis thos na bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed par 'gyur ba dang / bcom ldan 'das
4b7(sna tshogs): de bzhin gshegs pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'di zhus pa'i lan btab pas/ sems can thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed par 'gyur ba'i slad du/ de bzhin gshegs
5a1(sna tshogs): pa'i yul dang de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes bstan du gsol/ bcom ldan 'das bdag ni sems can dman pa la mos pa rnams kyi slad du/ de bzhin
5a2(sna tshogs): gshegs pa la zhu ba ma lags/ dbul ba'i sems dang ldan pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ dbul po'i theg pa la yang dag par zhugs pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ le lo
5a3(sna tshogs): can rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ le lo'i zil gyis non pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ lta ba'i 'dam du bying ba rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ bdud kyi zhags pas zin pa rnams
5a4(sna tshogs): kyi slad du ma lags/ ngo tsha ma 'tshal cing khrel ma mchis pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ yo byad bsnyungs pa dang mi ldan pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ bsgyung ngas pa rnams kyi slar
5a5(sna tshogs): du ma lags/ sems 'khrul pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ 'dod pa'i 'dam du bying ba rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ g.yon can rnams kyi snang du ma lags/ sgyu can rnams
5a6(sna tshogs): kyi slad du ma lags/ bgyis pa mi gzo ba rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ sdig pa 'tshal ba rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ sdig pa spyod pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ tshul khrims
5a7(sna tshogs): nyams pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ tshul khrims yongs su ma dag pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ lta ba nyams pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ bdud kyi spyod yul la spyod
5b1(sna tshogs): pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ bdag la bstod pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ gzhan la smod pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ rnyed pa dang bkur sti la gdu ba rnams kyi slad du ma lags
5b2(sna tshogs): lhung bzed dang chos gos la chags pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ tshul 'chos pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ kha gsag can rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ gzhogs slongs can rnams kyi
5b3(sna tshogs): slad du ma lags/ thob kyis 'jal ba rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ rnyed pa la rnyed par sgrub pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ bcom ldan 'das sems can de lta bu rnams kyi slad du
5b4(sna tshogs): bdag de bzhin gshegs pa la zhu ba ma lags so/ / bcom ldan 'das sems can gang dag thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes tshol ba dang / chags pa ma mchis pa'i ye shes dang / rang
5b5(sna tshogs): byung gi ye shes dang / mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pa'i ye shes dang / bla na med pa'i ye shes tshol ba de dag dang / gang dag bdag dang pha rol kyang mi dmigs na/ bdag la bstod pa dang
5b6(sna tshogs): gzhan la smod pa lta ga la mchi ste/ bcom ldan 'das rwa bcad pa lta bur nga rgyal ma mchis pa/ zug rngu phyung ba/ gdol bu lta bur sems dman pa/ sems sa dang / chu dang /
5b7(sna tshogs): me dang / rlung dang / nam mkha' dang mtshungs pa'i sems can rnams dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi slad du/ bdag de bzhin gshegs pa la zhu lags
6a1(sna tshogs): so/ bcom ldan 'das gang dag chos kyang mi dmigs shing / rlom sems su mi bgyid la/ mngon par zhen pa ma mchis na/ chos ma lags pa lta ga la
6a2(sna tshogs): mchis te/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag gi slad du/ bdag de bzhin gshegs pa la zhu lags so// bcom ldan 'das bsam pa dag pa/ g.yo ma mchis
6a3(sna tshogs): pa/ sgyu ma mchis pa/ drang ba/ sems mnyam pa/ sems can thams cad la sman pa dang / snying brtse ba can yang dag par 'dzin du stsol ba/ yang dag par gzengs
6a4(sna tshogs): bstod pa/ yang dag par dga' bar bgyid pa/ khur chen po khyer ba/ theg pa chen po la mngon par zhugs pa/ bgyi ba chen pos so sor nye bar gnas pa/ snying rje chen po dang
6a5(sna tshogs): ldan pa/ sems can thams cad bde ba thob par bgyid pa/ 'dren pa/ rnam par 'dren pa/ yongs su 'dren pa/ chos thams cad la mi rten par gnas pa/ skye ba'i gnas
6a6(sna tshogs): thams cad mi tshol ba/ bdud kyi zhags pa thams cad las rnam par grol ba/ 'dun pa can/ brtson 'grus dang ldan pa/ bag mchis pa/ chos thams cad kyi dam pa'i
6a7(sna tshogs): pha rol tu phyin pa/ the tshom thams cad gcod pa la mkhas pa'i sems can rnams dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi slad du/ bcom ldan 'das
6b1(sna tshogs): bdag de bzhin gshegs pa la zhu lags so/ / bcom ldan 'das sems can gang dag sangs rgyas kyi ye shes la'ang rlom sems su mi bgyid cing / mngon par mi zhen la/ chags
6b2(sna tshogs): par mi gnas shing / rlom sems thams cad las yang dag par 'das pa'i lam la gnas par lam du zhugs pa/ lam ston pa'i sems can rnams dang / byang chub sems dpa'
6b3(sna tshogs): sems dpa' chen po de dag gi slad du/ bcom ldan 'das bdag de bzhin gshegs pa la zhu lags so// bcom ldan 'das bdag ni sems can thams cad la bde ba dang / lhag
6b4(sna tshogs): na ma mchis pa'i bde ba dang / bla na ma mchis pa'i bde ba dang / mya ngan las 'das pa'i bde ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi bde ba dang / 'dus ma bgyis pa'i bde ba nye bar bsgrub par
6b5(sna tshogs): 'tshal te/ bdag sems can thams cad kyi don dang / sman pa dang / bde ba dang / grub pa dang / bde ba'i slad du/ de bzhin gshegs pa la zhu lags so// bcom
6b6(sna tshogs): ldan 'das bdag ni the tshom ma mchis par 'tshal zhing / the tsom mchis nas kyang / sems can rnams kyi the tsom rab tu spong ba'i slad du/ chos bshad par 'tshal te/ bcom
6b7(sna tshogs): ldan 'das bdag sems can thams cad kyi the tsom bsal ba'i slad du/ bcom ldan 'das la zhu lags so// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das sems can thams cad ni
7a1(sna tshogs): sdug bsngal dang mi mthun zhing / bde ba 'tshal la/ sems can thams cad ni bde ba don du gnyer ba lags te/ bcom ldan 'das shes rab ma gtogs
7a2(sna tshogs): par/ gzhan sems can rnams kyi bde ba gang yang bdag gis ma mthong zhing / bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa/ theg pa chen po ma gtogs par/ sems
7a3(sna tshogs): can rnams kyi bde ba gang yang ma mchis te/ bcom ldan 'das bdag gis don gyi dbang 'di mthong bas/ sems can rnams la bde ba nye bar bsgrub pa'i slad du/ shes rab kyi pha
7a4(sna tshogs): rol tu phyin pa zhu lags so/ / bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi don 'di yang dag par mthong bas/ bdag gis de bzhin gshegs pa la don 'di zhu lags so//
7a5(sna tshogs): de skad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to//
7a6(sna tshogs): rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa legs so legs so// khyod skye bo phal po che la snying brtse ba'i phyir/ de bzhin gshegs pa la shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'di 'dri ba ni khyod kyi yon
7a7(sna tshogs): tan gyi mtha' gtogs par sla ba ma yin no/ / de'i phyir rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa legs par nyon la rab tu yid la zung zhig dang / ngas khyod la bshad do// bcom ldan 'das
7b1(sna tshogs): legs so zhes gsol nas/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ bcom ldan 'das kyi ltar nyan pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis
7b2(sna tshogs): 'di skad ces bka' stsal to/ / rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa khyod 'di skad du/ bcom ldan 'das khyod shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bgyi ba
7b3(sna tshogs): bcom ldan 'das ji tsam gyis na byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bgyi zhes zer ba ni/ rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu
7b4(sna tshogs): phyin pa ni/ chos gang gis kyang brjod par bya ba ma yin te/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni/ tshig thams cad las 'das pa'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ shes
7b5(sna tshogs): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni/ 'di shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// 'dis shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// de'i phyir shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o zhes brjod par mi nus so//
7b6(sna tshogs): rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ 'di chos thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yin te/ de'i phyir shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/
7b7(sna tshogs): shes rab nyid kyang de bzhin gshegs pas ma rnyed ma dmigs na/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa lta dmigs par ga la 'gyur/ rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ shes
8a1(sna tshogs): rab ces bya ba 'di ni chos thams cad kun tu shes pa/ 'di ni chos thams cad kun tu rig pa ste/ de'i phyir shes rab ces bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par
8a2(sna tshogs): gnon pa/ chos thams cad kun tu rig pa gang zhe na/ chos 'di dag thams cad ni rnam pa gzhan na/ chos thams cad rnam pa gzhan du brjod de/ chos thams cad ni brjod pa
8a3(sna tshogs): las rnam par grol ba ma yin no/ / gang chos thams cad kun tu shes pa dang / gang chos thams cad kun tu rig pa de'ang tshig gis brjod par mi nus mod kyi/ 'on kyang ji ltar
8a4(sna tshogs): sems can rnams kyis shes par gyur pa de ltar shes rab ces bya'o/ / 'di ni btags pa zhes bya ste/ de'i phyir shes rab ces bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa
8a5(sna tshogs): chos thams cad ni gdags su med/ gzung du med/ bshad du med/ snang ba med de/ de lta bur kun tu rig pa de ni kun tu rig pa zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon
8a6(sna tshogs): pa shes rab ces bya ba de ni shes pa'ang ma yin/ kun tu mi shes pa'ang ma yin/ de las kyang ma yin/ de las ma yin pa'ang ma yin te/ de'i phyir shes rab ces bya'o//
8a7(sna tshogs): rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ de ni mi shes pa'i spyod yul yang ma yin/ ye shes kyi spyod yul yang ma yin/ mi shes pa'i yul yang ma yin/ ye shes kyi yul yang
8b1(sna tshogs): ma yin te/ ye shes ni yul med pa'o// gal te ye shes la yul yod du zin na mi shes par 'gyur ro// ye shes ni mi shes pa las ma yin/ mi shes pa'ang ye shes las ma
8b2(sna tshogs): yin/ ye shes ni mi shes pa ma yin/ mi shes pa'ang ye shes ma yin te/ ye shes kyis ye shes shes bya'o// ye shes kyis mi shes pa zhes mi bya'o// mi shes pas ye shes
8b3(sna tshogs): shes bya'o/ / de la ye shes ni 'di'o// ye shes de ni 'di'i 'o// ye shes de ni 'dis so// ye shes de ni 'di'i phyir ro zhes ye shes cung zad kyang bstan par mi nus te/ de'i phyir
8b4(sna tshogs): ye shes de ni ye shes nyid kyis med do/ / ye shes kyang ye shes su mi gnas te/ mi shes pas kyang ye shes shes mi bya'o// gal te mi shes pa ye shes shes bya na ni/ de'i phyir
8b5(sna tshogs): byis pa so so'i skye bo thams cad kyang ye shes can du 'gyur ro/ / gang ye shes dang mi shes pa mi dmigs shing / ye shes dang mi shes pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su shes pa
8b6(sna tshogs): de nyid ye shes shes bya ste/ ye shes ni ji skad du brjod pa de bzhin du ma yin no// de bas na ye shes ni brjod par bya ba ma yin zhing / yul thams cad las rab tu 'das pa ste/
8b7(sna tshogs): ye shes ni gang gi yul yang ma yin no// ye shes kyi yul yang gang yang ma yin no// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ ye shes bstan pa'i yul yang ma yin/ phyogs
9a1(sna tshogs): kyang ma yin pa 'di gang gis shes pa de ni ye shes can nam/ ye shes can ma yin pa zhes bya ba'i grangs su mi 'gro'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/
9a2(sna tshogs): gang 'di ltar rab tu shes pa dang / rjes su rtogs pa dang / kun tu shes pa de ni shes rab ces bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ gang 'di ltar mngon par rtogs pa
9a3(sna tshogs): mngon sum du byed pa de ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab ces bya'o/ / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab ces ji skad du brjod pa bzhin du ni ma yin no// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'jig
9a4(sna tshogs): rten nyid kyang mi dmigs na/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab lta ga la yod de/ 'jig rten 'das pa'i shes rab kyis/ gang 'jig rten las sgrol bar 'gyur ba lta ci smos
9a5(sna tshogs): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ des 'jig rten mi dmigs pas/ ci'ang sgrol bar mi byed de/ de'i phyir 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab ces bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa
9a6(sna tshogs): 'jig rten zhes bya ba 'di ni btags pa zhes brjod pa ste/ btags pa ni 'jig rten las yang dag par 'das pa ma yin gyi/ btags pa thams cad las yang dag par 'das pa ni
9a7(sna tshogs): 'jig rten las 'das pa zhes bya'o/ / 'da' bar bya ba ni 'jig rten las 'das pa ma yin gyi/ 'da' bar mi bya ba ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de la gang
9b1(sna tshogs): 'da' bar bya ba dang / gang gis 'da' bar bya ba'i chos phra rab tsam yang med pas/ de'i phyir 'das pa zhes bya ste/ 'jig rten las 'das pa la ni 'jig rten yang med/ 'jig rten
9b2(sna tshogs): las 'das pa'ang med do/ / bla na med pa la ni bsgral ba med de/ de'i phyir 'jig rten las 'das pa zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ 'di ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i
9b3(sna tshogs): shes rab bstan pa zhes bya ste/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab ces ji skad du brjod pa bzhin du ni ma yin no// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'jig rten las 'das pa ni brjod par bya ba ma
9b4(sna tshogs): yin gyi/ de ni brgal ba ste/ de la ni 'da' bar bya ba ci'ang med pas/ de'i phyir 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab ces bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ de la
9b5(sna tshogs): gang nges par rtogs pa'i shes rab des ci nges par rtogs/ 'di la ni nges par rtogs par bya ba ci'ang med do// gal te nges par rtogs par bya ba 'ga' zhig yod du zin na ni/ 'di
9b6(sna tshogs): shes rab kyis nges par rtogs pa zhes gdags na/ gang gis kyang mi rtogs shing / kun rtogs pa ma yin la/ kun rtogs par 'gyur ba'i bye brag gang yang mi dmigs so//
9b7(sna tshogs): nges par rtogs pa zhes bya ba ni/ 'di la rtogs par byed pa ci'ang med cing / kun tu rtogs par bya ba'ang med de/ de la rtogs par byed pa ci'ang med cing / kun tu rtogs par
10a1(sna tshogs): bya ba'ang med pas/ de'i phyir nges par rtogs pa zhes bya'o// 'di la ni gang yang mthar 'gro ba med cing / dbus su'ang ma yin te/ de'i phyir nges par rtogs pa
10a2(sna tshogs): zhes bya'o/ / nges par rtogs pa'i shes rab kyis rtogs pa ni steng ma rtogs te/ gang du'ang mi rgyug/ rnam par mi rgyug/ kun tu mi rgyug ste/ de'i phyir nges par rtogs pa zhes bya'o//
10a3(sna tshogs): rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ nges par rtogs shes bya ba'i shes rab kyis/ ci nges par rtogs she na/ gang ci snang ba de thams cad nges par rtogs so// gang gis nges
10a4(sna tshogs): par rtogs she na/ shes rab kyis so// shes rab kyis ji ltar nges par rtogs she na/ gang btags pa'i mtshan nyid de thams cad mtshan nyid med pa dang / mtshan nyid med pa'ang
10a5(sna tshogs): btags pa'i mtshan nyid du'o/ / rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ gang 'di lta bu'i shes rab dang ldan pas nges par rtogs pa des ni/ khams gsum rtogs so// ji ltar
10a6(sna tshogs): rtogs she na/ khams gsum ni khams med par rtogs te/ 'di la ni khams rtogs pa ci'ang med do// des khams gsum ni khams med par rtogs so// gang de ltar khams
10a7(sna tshogs): gsum khams med par nges par rtogs pa dang / gang gis de ltar khams gsum nges par rtogs pa de ni/ nges par rtogs pa'i shes rab dang ldan pa zhes bya'o// ji ltar na nges
10b1(sna tshogs): par rtogs pa'i shes rab dang ldan zhe na/ nges par rtogs par bya ba ni/ mi dge ba gang yang med de/ de thams cad dge bar nges par rtogs te/ de nges par rtogs pa'i shes rab
10b2(sna tshogs): kyis rab tu 'da' 'o/ / de de ltar rtogs pa'i shes rab dang ldan pas gang ci mthong ba dang / thos pa dang / mnams pa dang / myangs pa dang / reg pa dang / rnam par
10b3(sna tshogs): shes pa de dag thams cad nges par rtogs so/ / ji lta bur rtogs she na/ mi rtag pa dang / sdug bsngal ba dang / 'bras dang / nang dang / zug rngu dang / stong pa nyid dang /
10b4(sna tshogs): sdig pa dang / gnod pa dang / mtha' ma dang / 'jig pa dang / 'jig pa'i chos nyid dang / g.yo ba dang / 'jig pa'i tshul can dang / bdag med pa dang / mi skye ba dang //
10b5(sna tshogs): mi 'gog pa dang / mtshan nyid med par te/ rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ de ni bsil bar gyur pa/ zug rngu med pa zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/
10b6(sna tshogs): 'di lta ste/ dper na zug rngu med pa zhes bya ba'i sman gyi rigs de gang na 'dug pa de ni zug rngu thams cad sel cing nges par 'don to// de bzhin du 'di lta bu'i chos rnams dang ldan pa'i
10b7(sna tshogs): dge slong ni zug rngu med cing bsil bar gyur la/ nges par rtogs pa'i shes rab dang ldan zhing dug med la rtag tu gnas la/ nges par rtogs pa'i shes rab kyis khams gsum
11a1(sna tshogs): thams cad la mi chags shing / bdud kyi zhags pa thams cad las rab tu 'das so// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ 'di lta ste/ dper/
11a2(sna tshogs): na rdo rje ni dbug pa'i phyir gang du btsugs pa de dang de nyid du nges par phigs so// de bzhin du dge slong gis nges par rtogs pa'i shes rab kyis yongs su zin pa'i rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge
11a3(sna tshogs): 'dzin gang du btsugs pa dang / gang du spyod pa de dag thams cad nges par rtogs so// de nges par rtogs pa'i shes rab 'jig rten las 'das pa yang dag par sdug bsngal zad
11a4(sna tshogs): par 'gyur ba dang ldan pas/ chags pa med pa ni gsum rig pa zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ rig pa zhes bya ba de ni ma rig pa nye bar zhi ba'i tshig bla dgra
11a5(sna tshogs): so/ ma rig pa yongs su shes pa zhes bya ba de ni sdug bsngal gyi phung po nye bar zhi ba'i tshig bla dgas so// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ 'di lta ste/ dper na sman pa
11a6(sna tshogs): mkhas pa/ gsal ba/ yid rno ba/ lhag par rtog pa dang ldan pa/ sman thams cad la mkhas pa/ nad ldang ba thams cad la mkhas pa/ sdug bsngal thams
11a7(sna tshogs): cad las rnam par 'grel pa des nad pa gang dang gang la gso ba byas pa de dang de 'tsho'o/ / de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar de sman thams cad la mkhas shing / nang ldang ba thams
11b1(sna tshogs): cad la mkhas te/ nang thams cad las thar par byed pa'i phyir ro// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ de bzhin du rig pa gsum pos ni ma rig pa thams cad nye bar zhi bar
11b2(sna tshogs): 'gyur/ sdug bsngal tham cad 'joms par 'gyur/ rga shi dang / mya ngan dang / smre sngags 'don pa dang / sdug bsngal ba dang / yid mi bde ba dang / 'khrug pa
11b3(sna tshogs): thams cad nye bar zhi bar 'gyur te/ rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ de ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab nges par rtogs pa'i 'gro ba zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis
11b4(sna tshogs): rnam par gnon pa/ ngas 'di la dgongs nas/ srid par skye ba yongs zad par// gang gis yang dag rab shes pa// gang rnams rtogs par 'gro ba de// 'jig rten na ni shes
11b5(sna tshogs): rab mchog/ ces bshad do// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ srid par skye ba yongs su zad pa zhes bya ba gang gi tshig bla dag sa yin zhe na/ de ni 'byung ba dang nub pa rab
11b6(sna tshogs): tu rtogs pa'i tshig bla dgas so/ / 'byung ba dang nub pa gang zhe na/ kun 'byung ba'i chos ci'ang rung ste/ de thams cad ni 'gog pa'i chos te/ 'di ltar kun 'byung ba dang nub
11b7(sna tshogs): pa rab tu rtogs so/ / rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ kun 'byung ba zhes bya ba de ni 'byung ba'i tshig bla dgas so// nub pa zhes bya ba de ni 'gog pa'i tshig bla dgas te/
12a1(sna tshogs): 'byung ba dang nub pa zhes ji skad du brjod pa de bzhin du ni ma yin no// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ kun 'byung ba gang ci'ang rung ste/ de ni kun 'byung
12a2(sna tshogs): ba'i chos ma yin no/ / rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ mnyam pa las 'byung ba gang yang med de/ de ni kun 'byung bar mi 'gyur ro// de mnyam pa nyid kyi rjes su song ste//
12a3(sna tshogs): de'i phyir kun 'byung ba zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ mnyam pa'i rjes su song ba zhes bya ba ni/ 'di la 'byung ba gang yang med de/ kun 'byung bar yang mi
12a4(sna tshogs): 'gyur ro/ / de'i rang bzhin gang yin pa de ni/ rang gi ngang gis 'jig cing / de ni 'gog pa ste/ de la ni 'gog pa gang yang med do// mnyam pa ni bla na med pa'i 'gog pa ste//
12a5(sna tshogs): gang la skye ba med pa de la 'gog pa med de/ de ni 'gog pa'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ de ltar skye ba med cing 'gog pa med pa'i phyir gang 'byung ba dang nub pa rtogs
12a6(sna tshogs): pa de nub pa rab tu rtogs pa ste/ de'i phyir 'byung ba dang nub pa rab tu rtogs pa zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ rab tu rtogs shes bya ba de ni rten cing 'brel par
12a7(sna tshogs): 'byung ba yongs su shes pa zhes bya'o/ / gang brten nas chos gang skye ba de nyid la brten nas chos de med de/ 'di ni rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba rab tu rtogs pa zhes bya'o// rab kyi
12b1(sna tshogs): rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ de ni rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i yang dag pa nyid ji lta ba bzhin du skye ba med par bstan to// mi skye ba ni rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba ste/ mi
12b2(sna tshogs): 'byung ba mnyam pas/ de'i phyir rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba zhes bya'o// gang skye ba med pa de la 'gog pa ga la yod de/ 'gog pa dang mi 'gal ba de ni rten cing 'bral bar
12b3(sna tshogs): 'byung ba'i 'gog pa med pa ste/ skye ba med pa de ni rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba zhes bya'o// gang 'brel par 'byung ba de ni ma byung ba'o// gang ma byung ba de ni 'das pa ma yin/
12b4(sna tshogs): ma 'ongs pa ma yin/ da ltar byung ba ma yin/ gang 'das pa ma yin/ ma 'ongs pa ma yin/ da ltar byung ba ma yin pa de la 'gog pa med do// gang la 'gog pa med pa de
12b5(sna tshogs): ni mi skye ba shes pa zhes bya'o/ / gang gis mi skye bar shes pa de ni yang skyed pa ma yin/ 'gog pa mngon sum du byed pa'ang ma yin no// gang mi skyed pa de 'gog par mi byed de/ skye
12b6(sna tshogs): ba yin na ni 'gog par yang shes so/ / gang mi skyed pa des chos thams cad 'gog pa nyid du shes shing mthong la/ rab tu rtogs shing mngon sum du byas te/ de'i phyir 'gog pa
12b7(sna tshogs): mngon sum du byas pa zhes bya'o/ / zad pa shes pa zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ mi shes pa zad pa de'i phyir zad pa shes pa zhes bya'o// gang gis zad ce na
13a1(sna tshogs): mi zad pas zad de/ de'i zad pa'ang mi mthong ngo // rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ mi shes pa med pas/ de'i phyir de zad pa shes pa zhes bya'o//
13a2(sna tshogs): rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ mi shes pa yongs su shes pa de'i phyir mi shes pa zad de zad pa shes pa zhes bya'o// mi shes pa ni zad pa'am/ ma zad pa ma yin te/ 'di ni
13a3(sna tshogs): shes pa dang bral ba'i phyir zad pa shes pa zhes bya'o/ / rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ 'di ni yang dag pa'i lta ba bzhin du yongs su shes pa ste/ de'i phyir bral ba zhes bya'o//
13a4(sna tshogs): mi shes pa dang bral ba dang / shes pa dang bral ba 'di las gzhan ci'ang mi dmigs so// ye shes nyid kyang mi dmigs na/ gang zad pa las rnam par grol ba mi shes pa lnga'i
13a5(sna tshogs): smos te/ de'i phyir zad pa shes pa zhes bya'o// ji skad du brjod pa bzhin du ma yin no// zad pa gang yin pa de la tha snyad du gdags pa gang yang med mod kyi/ 'on kyang 'di ltar
13a6(sna tshogs): mi shes pa zad pa dang / zad pa shes pa zhes bstan to// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ gang gis chos thams cad mi zad pa dang / zad pa shes pa la brtag pa
13a7(sna tshogs): khong du chud pa de zad pa shes pa dang bral te/ zad pa med pa'i mtha' rjes su thob bo// mtha' med pa ni mya ngan las 'das pa'i mtha' ste/ ji skad du brjod pa bzhin du ni ma
13b1(sna tshogs): yin no/ / chos thams cad ni mya ngan las 'das pa'i mtha' ste/ mtha' med pa'o// mtha' thams cad chad pa ni mya ngan las 'das pa'i mtha' zhes bya ste/ ji skad du brjod pa
13b2(sna tshogs): bzhin du ni ma yin no/ / mya ngan las 'das pa ni tha snyad thams cad chad pa/ brjod par bya ba ma yin pa ste/ rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings
13b3(sna tshogs): bstan pa 'di'ang ji skad du bstan pa bzhin du ni ma yin no/ / bstan pa thams cad las yang dag par 'das pas/ mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings ni bstan du med de/ bstan pa
13b4(sna tshogs): thams cad rab tu chad pa de ni mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings shes bya'o/ / mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings shes bya ba gang yin pa de ni/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab nges par
13b5(sna tshogs): rtogs pa bstan pa la bya'o/ / rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings de ni yul na mi gnas/ phyogs na mi gnas pa zhes bstan to// rab kyi
13b6(sna tshogs): rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ de la shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa gang zhe na/ rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la tshu rol lam/ pha rol gang
13b7(sna tshogs): yang med do/ / rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ gal te shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la tshu rol lam/ pha rol dmigs na ni de bzhin gshegs pas shes rab kyi pha rol
14a1(sna tshogs): tu phyin pa'i tshu rol lam/ pha rol bshad pa zhig na/ rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshu rol mi dmigs pas/ de'i
14a2(sna tshogs): phyir de'i pha rol kyang med mod kyi/ 'on kyang rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya ba de ni chos thams cad kyi pha rol lo// de'i phyir shes rab kyi pha rol
14a3(sna tshogs): tu phyin pa zhes bya ste/ ji skad du brjod pa bzhin du ni ma yin no// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni tshig dang las kyis nye bar gnas pa ma yin
14a4(sna tshogs): teshes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni bstan du med pa'o/ / chos thams cad de ltar khong du chud na/ de ni ji lta ba bzhin du khong du chud de mi 'gal lo// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de la
14a5(sna tshogs): khong du chud pa ci'ang med cing / rab tu rtogs pa'ang med pa'i phyir ro// khong du chud pa dang / rab tu rtogs pa mnyam pa nyid ni byang chub ste/ chos thams cad khong du chud pa ni byang
14a6(sna tshogs): chub ces bya'o/ / ji ltar chos thams cad khong du chud ce na/ 'di la byang chub gang yang med/ 'di khong du chud pa gang yang med de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam
14a7(sna tshogs): par gnon pa/ gal te byang chub dmigs na ni/ byang chub la'ang byang chub dmigs par 'gyur ro// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ byang chub la ni byang chub med de/
14b1(sna tshogs): de ltar byang chub 'di mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar bya'o// khong du chud ba med pa dang / rab tu rtogs pa med pas rjes su rtogs pa zhes bya ste/ ji skad du brjod pa bzhin du ni
14b2(sna tshogs): ma yin no/ / chos thams cad ni khong du chud pa ma yin/ rab tu rtogs pa ma yin te/ chos ni chos kyi ngo bo nyid kyis med do// de ltar khong du chud pa de ni byang chub ces bya'o//
14b3(sna tshogs): rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ de bzhin gshegs pas ni byang chub ma dmigs shing / de bzhin gshegs pas ni byang chub rnam par ma rig ste/ byang chub ni rnam par
14b4(sna tshogs): rig par bya ba ma yin/ rab tu rnam par rig par bya ba ma yin no// de bzhin gshegs pas ni byang chub ma mkhyen ma bskyed de/ byang chub ni ma skyes shing mngon par ma grub bo//
14b5(sna tshogs): byang chub ni su'i yang ma yin zhing / byang chub la sems can nam/ sems can du gdags pa gang yang med do// gang la sems can nam/ sems can du gdags pa med pa
14b6(sna tshogs): de la 'di byang chub sems dpa'/ 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes ji ltar brjod/ rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ byang chub la byang chub
14b7(sna tshogs): kyang med/ byang chub la sems can yang med de/ byang chub 'di ni shin tu 'das pa'o// byang chub 'di ni ma skyes pa'o// byang chub 'di ni mngon par ma grub pa'o// byang
15a1(sna tshogs): chub 'di ni mtshan nyid med pa ste/ 'di la sems can med cing mi dmigs so// byang chub ni sems can gyis btagasu bu ma yin gyi/ sems can
15a2(sna tshogs): med par khong du chud pa ni byang chub ces bya'o/ / byang chub sems can ma yin par gang gis shes pa de byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rab kyi rtsal gyis
15a3(sna tshogs): rnam par gnon pa/ byang chub sems dpa' ni sems can gyi 'du shes kyis bskyed pa ma yin gyi/ sems can gyi 'du shes rnam par 'jig pa'i phyir ro// byang chub
15a4(sna tshogs): sems dpa' zhes bya ste/ ji skad du brjod pa bzhin du ni ma yin no// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa' ni brjod par bya ba ma yin zhing / byang chub sems
15a5(sna tshogs): dpa' ni sems can gyi rang bzhin dang bral ba'i phyir ro/ / byang chub ni sems can du 'du shes pa dang bral ba ste/ gang gis byang chub de ltar shes pa byang chub sems dpa'
15a6(sna tshogs): zhes bya'o/ / byang chub ji lta bur shes she na/ byang chub 'di ni shin tu 'das pa'o// byang chub 'di ni bya ba ma yin pa'o// byang chub 'di ni skye ba med pa/ 'gog pa med
15a7(sna tshogs): pa'o/ / byang chub ni byang chub kyis shes par mi byed/ byang chub ni rnam par shes par bya ba ma yin/ rnam par rig par bya ba ma yin/ gdags par bya ba ma yin te/
15b1(sna tshogs): mngon par ma grub pa ni byang chub ces bya'o// rnam par mi rtog pa dang / rtog pa bcad pa'i phyir/ gang gis khong du chud pa dag rab tu rtogs pa de'i phyir/ byang chub sems
15b2(sna tshogs): dpa' zhes bya ste/ 'di skad du brjod pa bzhin du ma yin no// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ sems can med pa'i phyir ro// gal te byang chub sems dpa' yang dag par dmigs na ni//
15b3(sna tshogs): 'di ni byang chub/ 'di ni sems can zhes byang chub de'ang rnyed par 'gyur ro// sems can med pa dang / sems can ma yin pa dang / sems can dang bral bar khong du chud pa
15b4(sna tshogs): ni byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya'o/ / sems can med pa dang / sems can du 'du shes rnam par bshig nas/ byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/
15b5(sna tshogs): sems can gyi khams shes bya ba de ni/ sems can med pa'i tshig bla dwags so// sems can gyi khams med pa'i phyir/ sems can la sems can med do// gal te
15b6(sna tshogs): sems can la sems can yod na ni/ sems can gyi khams shes mi bya'o// sems can gyi khams shes bya ba de ni/ khams med par bstan te/ khams med pa ni
15b7(sna tshogs): sems can gyi khams so/ / gal te sems can gyi khams sems can gyi khams su gyur na ni/ srog de lus de yin par 'gyur ro// ci ste sems can gyi khams rnam par
16a1(sna tshogs): grol ba khams gsum du gyur na ni/ srog kyang gzhan/ lus kyang gzhan du 'gyur ro// khams med pa ni sems can gyi khams te/ brdas tha snyad
16a2(sna tshogs): du gdags pa'i tshig tu 'gro'o/ / sems can gyi khams la ni khams med de/ khams ma rtogs pas sems can gyi khams med do// chos thams cad ni khams med pa ste/
16a3(sna tshogs): ngas de la dgongs nas/ sems can gyi khams ni gang ba 'am/ bri bar yang mi mngon no zhes bshad do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ sems can gyi khams rab tu dben pa'i phyir/
16a4(sna tshogs): sems can gyi khams ni sems can ma yin no// ji ltar sems can gyi khams bri ba dang gang bar mi mngon pa bzhin du/ chos thams cad kyang bri ba 'am/ gang bar mi mngon
16a5(sna tshogs): no/ gang dag bri ba 'am/ gang bar 'gyur bar chos thams cad la yongs su grub pa gang yang med de/ gang gis de ltar chos thams cad khong du chud pa de ni/ sangs
16a6(sna tshogs): rgyas kyi chos khong du chud pa zhes bya ste/ ngas 'di la dgongs nas/ ji ltar sems can gyi khams bri ba 'am/ gang bar mi mngon pa de bzhin du/ chos thams
16a7(sna tshogs): cad kyang bri ba 'am/ gang bar mi mngon no zhes bya ba bshad do// gang yang yongs su ma grub pa'i tshul gyis/ chos thams cad bri ba ma yin/ gang ba ma yin pa
16b1(sna tshogs): des/ sangs rgyas kyi chos kyang bri ba ma yin/ gang ba ma yin no// de ltar chos thams cad khong du chud pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams bri ba med cing / gang ba
16b2(sna tshogs): med pa'o/ / chos thams cad bri ba med cing / gang ba med pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi chos shes bya ba de ni/ sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi tshig bla dgas ma yin no// sangs
16b3(sna tshogs): rgyas kyi chos ni gang gis kyang bri ba 'am/ gang bar bya bar mi nus so// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ni chos thams cad khong du chud pa'i phyir te/ gang chos thams cad khong du
16b4(sna tshogs): chud pa de la bri ba 'am/ gang ba'i chos ci'ang med do// chos thams cad ces bya ba de ni chos kyi dbyings kyi tshig bla dgas te/ chos kyi dbyings la bri ba 'am/ gang ba med
16b5(sna tshogs): do/ / de ci'i phyir zhe na/ chos kyi dbyings ni mtha' yas pa'i phyir ro// sems can gyi khams dang chos kyi dbyings ni tha dad du mi dmigs so// sems can gyi khams dang chos
16b6(sna tshogs): kyi dbyings bri ba 'am/ gang bar dmigs pa 'am/ yod pa ma yin te/ gang gis de ltar khong du chud pa de ni byang chub ces bya'o// de'i phyir sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams bri ba
16b7(sna tshogs): 'am gang bar mi mngon zhes bya'o/ / rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ bri ba med cing / gang ba med pa zhes ji skad du smra ba de ni/ brtag pa yang dag pa ji lta ba
17a1(sna tshogs): bzhin du mthong ba'i tshig bla dwags so/ / de la ci'ang bsal ba 'am/ gzhag par mi nus te/ gang de ltar khong du chud pa de ni byang chub ces bya'o// rab kyi rtsal
17a2(sna tshogs): gyis rnam par gnon pa/ byang chub ces bya ba de ni sangs rgyas kyi mtshan nyid do// sangs rgyas kyi mtshan nyid ji lta bu zhe na/ chos thams cad kyi mtshan nyid/ mtshan nyid med pa de ni
17a3(sna tshogs): sangs rgyas kyi mtshan nyid do/ / byang chub ni mtshan nyid med pa ste/ mtshan nyid kyi rang bzhin las bzlog pa'o// gang de ltar khong du chud pa de ni byang chub ces bya ste/ ji skad du brjod
17a4(sna tshogs): pa bzhin du ni ma yin no/ / rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ de ni chos thams cad rjes su rtogs pas/ byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par
17a5(sna tshogs): gnon pa/ gang la la zhig chos 'di rab tu mi shes/ khong du ma chud par/ bdag byang chub sems dpa' zhes khas 'chen/ de ni byang chub sems dpa'i sa las ring ngo //
17a6(sna tshogs): de ni byang chub sems dpa'i chos rnams las ring ngo // de ni byang chub sems dpa'i ming gis lha dang / mi dang / lha ma yin dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten la bslu ba'o// rab kyi
17a7(sna tshogs): rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ byang chub sems dpar gyur na ni/ de'i phyir sems can thams cad kyang byang chub sems dpar 'gyur ro// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/
17b1(sna tshogs): 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa zhes bya ba de ni tshig gi las tsam ma yin no// tshig gis bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar
17b2(sna tshogs): nus so/ / tshig gi las kyi byang chub dang / byang chub sems dpa'i chos rnams thob par mi 'gyur ro// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ sems can thams cad ni byang
17b3(sna tshogs): chub la spyod mod kyi/ mi shes shing khong du ma chud de/ de'i phyir de dag byang chub sems dpa' zhes mi bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ sems can rnams sems can med par mi
17b4(sna tshogs): shes pa'i phyir ro/ / gal te de ltar shes na bdag gis spyod pa dag gis/ byang chub sems dpa' dag tu 'gyur ba'i rigs so// sems can thams cad ni phyin ci log pas rang
17b5(sna tshogs): gi spyod pa dang / rang gi yul dang / rang gi spyod yul rab tu mi shes so// gal te rang gi spyod pa rab tu shes na ni/ de dag slar gang la'ang rnam par rtog cing spyod par mi 'gyur/
17b6(sna tshogs): ro/ rnam par rtog pa dang spyod pa de dag gis byis pa so so'i skye bo thams cad yang dag par yin po la dmigs shing spyod kyang / de dag byang chub la dmigs pa snyam du rlom sems
17b7(sna tshogs): su byed de/ dmigs pa la spyod cing / rtog pa la spyod pa de dag la byang chub ga la yod/ byang chub sems dpa'i chos rnams ga la yod/ gang gis chos de lta bur
18a1(sna tshogs): rab tu shes pa de dag slar yang dag pa ma yin pa'i dmigs pa la mi spyod cing / de dag ni phyir chos gang yang rlom sems su mi byed de/ de'i phyir spyod pa med pa ni//
18a2(sna tshogs): byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa zhes bya'o// byang chub sems dpa' ni rtog pa dang rnam par rtog pa la mi spyod do// gang la rtog pa med pa de la spyod pa gang yang med do// gang la rnam
18a3(sna tshogs): par rtog pa med pa de la spyod pa'i don gang yang meng ngo / / sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod pa thams cad ni rnam par mi rtog par spyod cing / thams cad rlom
18a4(sna tshogs): sems med la/ dmigs pa dang bcas pa ma yin pa ste/ chos thams cad de ltar rab tu shes pa de ni/ phyir dmigs pa 'am/ rnam par rtog pa la spyod pa'am/
18a5(sna tshogs): rnam par spyod pa med de/ de ni spyod pa med pa'i tshul gyis/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod pa zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ de ltar na byang chub
18a6(sna tshogs): sems dpa' byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la spyod pa yin no/ / rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon po/ gang de ltar chos khong du chud cing / rab tu rtogs pa de'i phyir/ byang
18a7(sna tshogs): chub sems dpa' zhes bya'o/ / des sems can du 'du shes bsal bas/ sems can med pa zhes bya ba de ni/ byang chub sems dpa'i tshig bla dgas so// de ci'i phyir zhi
18b1(sna tshogs): na/ des sems can thams cad yang dag pa ma yin pa dang / sems can thams cad sems can ma yin pa dang / sems can thams cad ni phyin ci log gi sems can dang /
18b2(sna tshogs): sems can thams cad ni yongs su brtags pas sems can dang / sems can thams cad ni yod pa ma yin pa la dmigs pas sems can dang / sems can thams cad ni rang
18b3(sna tshogs): gis spyod pa rnam par ma rung bar byas pas sems can dang / sems can thams cad ni ma rig pa 'du byed pas sems can no zhes shes pa'i phyir ro// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ sems
18b4(sna tshogs): can thams cad ni chos gang dag med pa'i chos de dag mngon par 'du byed pas/ de'i phyir sems can thams cad ni ma rig pa 'du byed pas sems can zhes bya'o// chos med pa gang zhe na/
18b5(sna tshogs): nga zhe 'am/ nga'i zhe 'am/ nga'o zhes bya ba'i chos gang yang med pa'o// gal te chos 'ga' zhig nga zhe 'am/ nga'i zhe 'am/ nga'o zhes bya bar gyur na/ de'i phyir sems can
18b6(sna tshogs): thams cad yang dag par 'gyur ba zhig na/ rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ 'di ltar nga zhe 'am/ nga'i zhe 'am/ nga'o zhes bya ba'i chos gang yang med pas/ de'i phyir
18b7(sna tshogs): sems can ni yang dag pa ma yin pa ste/ sems can thams cad ni ma rig pa 'du byed pas sems can thams cad ces bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ gang la'ang
19a1(sna tshogs): nga zhe 'am/ nga'i zhe 'am/ nga'o zhes bya ba'i sems can zhes bya ba'i chos gang yang med de/ gang gi phyir med pa de'i phyir sems can ni yang dag pa ma yin pa
19a2(sna tshogs): zhes bya'o/ / yang dag pa ma yin pa zhes bya ba de ni sems can med pa'i tshig bla dgas so// ji ltar sems can du 'du shes pa yang dag pa ma yin pa la mngon par zhen pa de ltar sems
19a3(sna tshogs): can rnams yang dag pa ma yin pa zhes bya'o/ / rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ yang dag pa ma yin pa zhes bya ba de la ni yang dag pa ci'ang med cing ma byung ba'o// chos thams
19a4(sna tshogs): cad kyang yang dag pa ma yin zhing ma byung ba'o/ / de la sems can yang dag pa ma yin pa la lhag par chags pa de ni rnam par 'ching ba ste/ de'i phyir yang dag pa ma yin pa la dmigs
19a5(sna tshogs): ni sems can zhes bya'o/ / de dag ni spyod pa gang khong du chud pas/ byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya ba'i rang gi spyod pa de mi shes te/ yongs su ma rtogs pas sems can ni yang
19a6(sna tshogs): dag pa ma yin pa zhes bya'o/ / rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ gang de ltar khong du chud pa de ni byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya'o// byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya ba de ni/
19a7(sna tshogs): gang gis chos thams cad khong du chud cing shes la/ sems can rjes su rtogs pa'i tshig bla dgas so// ji ltar shes she na/ yang dag pa ma yin pa dang / mi byung ba pa
19b1(sna tshogs): phyin ci log ma yin par ro/ / ji ltar byis pa so so'i skye bo dag gis brtags pa de dag ni de bzhin du ma yin no// ji ltar byis pa so so'i skye bo dag gis rnyed pa de dag de bzhin du ma yin
19b2(sna tshogs): te/ de'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ byang chub ni ma brtags rnam par brtags shing / byang chub mngon par ma bsgrubs la/ mi dmigs pa'i
19b3(sna tshogs): phyir ro/ / rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ de bzhin gshegs pas ni byang chub ma brnyes so// chos thams cad mi rnyed cing / chos thams cad mi dmigs pa'i phyir byang
19b4(sna tshogs): chub ces bya'o/ / de lta bu ni sangs rgyas kyi byang chub ces bya ste/ ji skad du brjod pa bzhin du ni ma yin no// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ gang dag byang chub kyi phyir
19b5(sna tshogs): sems 'od bskyed par bya'o/ / zhes byang chub tu sems bskyed pa dang / gang du bdag gis sems bskyed par bya ba'i byang chub de yod do// zhes byang chub rlom sems su byed
19b6(sna tshogs): pa de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' zhes mi bya ste/ de dag ni sems can skyes pa zhes bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar de dag ni skye bar mngon par zhen cing
19b7(sna tshogs): sems su mngon par zhen nas/ byang chub la mngon par zhen pa'i phyir ro// gang dag byang chub kyi phyir sems bskyed pa de dag ni/ byang chub kyi sems la mngon par zhen pa
20a1(sna tshogs): zhes bya'o/ / gang gi phyir mngon par 'du byed pa de'i phyir/ byang chub tu sems bskyed de/ de bas na mngon par 'du byed pa ni sems can zhes bya ste/
20a2(sna tshogs): byang chub sems dpa' ma yin no// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de dag ni sems can skyes pa zhes bya ba'i phyir ro// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ byang chub ni ma skyes shing
20a3(sna tshogs): byang chub ni bsam du med pas/ byang chub kyi phyir sems par mi nus so// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ de dag ni skye ba nyid la mngon par zhen kyang / de dag skye ba rab tu
20a4(sna tshogs): mi shes so/ / rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ skye ba mnyam pa nyid gang yin pa de ni yang dag pa nyid do// sems mnyam pa nyid gang yin pa dang / yang dag pa nyid gang yin
20a5(sna tshogs): pa dang / mnyam pa nyid gang yin pa dang / yang dag pa nyid de ni byang chub ste/ gang na yang dag pa ji lta ba nyid yod pa de na/ rnam par rtog pa gang yang med na/ de dag ni
20a6(sna tshogs): sems dang byang chub la rnam par brtags te/ gnyis su mngon par zhen nas/ byang chub kyi phyir sems bskyed do// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ sems kyang
20a7(sna tshogs): gzhan ma yin/ byang chub kyang gzhan ma yin/ sems la byang chub med/ byang chub la'ang sems med de/ byang chub gang yin pa dang / sems gang yin pa de ni
20b1(sna tshogs): yang dag pa ji lta ba nyid dang / ji lta ba bzhin no// de la ni byang chub med/ sems kyang med do// gang gi sems nyid dang / byang chub dang / skye ba dang / mi skye ba'ang mi
20b2(sna tshogs): dmigs pa de byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya'o/ / yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin gyi sems dpa' zhes bya'o// sems dpa' chen po zhes bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ des yang
20b3(sna tshogs): dag pa ma yin pa gang yin pa de shes pa'i phyir ro/ / yang dag pa ma yin pa gang zhe na/ 'jig rten thams cad ni yang dag pa ma yin pa ste/ yang dag pa ma yin par gtogs so//
20b4(sna tshogs): kye ma 'jig rten gnas pa 'di ni yang dag pa ma yin pa'o// ma byung ba'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ yang dag pa ma yin pa/ mi 'byung ba zhes bya zhe na/ yang dag pa ma yin pa la
20b5(sna tshogs): 'byung ba gang yang med de/ yang dag pa ma yin pa ni mi 'byung ba'o// de'i phyir chos thams cad ngo bo nyid kyis med pa/ yang dag pa ma yin pa zhes bya'o// gang gis de ltar shes
20b6(sna tshogs): pa de ni/ yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin gyi sems can zhes bya'o// yang dag pa la yang dag pa zhes mngon par mi zhen pas/ de'i phyir yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin gyi sems can zhes bya ste/
20b7(sna tshogs): ji skad du brjod pa bzhin du ma yin no// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ yang dag pa ma yin pa la sems can nam/ sems can chen po zhes bya ba gang yang med pa'i phyir ro// gang gis theg pa
21a1(sna tshogs): chen po khong du chud pa de sems can chen po zhes bya'o/ / theg pa chen po gang zhe na/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes ni theg pa chen po'o// thams cad mkhyen pa'i
21a2(sna tshogs): ye shes gang zhe na/ gang ci'ang rung ste/ 'dus byas shes pa dang / 'dus ma byas shes pa dang / 'jig rten shes pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa shes pa des sems
21a3(sna tshogs): can chen po zhes bya'o/ / de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de sems can du 'du shes pa chen po med pas/ de'i phyir sems can chen po zhes bya'o// de la ma rig pa'i phung po chen po med pas
21a4(sna tshogs): de'i phyir sems can chen po zhes bya'o/ / de la 'du byed kyi phung po chen po med pas/ de'i phyir sems can chen po zhes bya'o// de la mi shes pa'i phung po chen po med pas/ de'i
21a5(sna tshogs): phyir sems can chen po zhes bya'o/ / de la sdug bsngal gyi phung po chen po med pas/ de'i phyir sems can chen po zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ gang dag
21a6(sna tshogs): sems dpa' chen po'i 'du shes la'ang smod la/ sems kyang mi dmigs/ sems las byung ba'i chos dang / sems kyi rang bzhin yang rab tu mi shes/ byang chub
21a7(sna tshogs): kyang mi dmigs/ byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos rnams dang / byang chub kyi rang bzhin yang rab tu mi shes te/ de dag mi shes pa'i sems kyis byang chub kyang mi mthong
21b1(sna tshogs): chub ma gtogs par sems kyang mi mthong / byang chub la sems mi mthong / sems la byang chub mi mthong ste/ gang de ltar rnam par 'jig pa de ni sgom pa'ang med/ rnam
21b2(sna tshogs): par 'jig par byed pa'ang med de/ rnam par 'jig par byed pa de'ang mi dmigs shing / rlom sems mi byed la/ mngon par zhen pa de dag byang chub tu sems bskyed do//
21b3(sna tshogs): rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ gang de ltar byang chub tu sems bskyed pa de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' yang dag pa zhes bya ste/ de dag byang chub las phyir mi
21b4(sna tshogs): ldog go/ / de ci'i phyir zhe na/ gang dag 'di ltar byang chub dang / sems dang / skye ba dang / 'gog pa tha dad du bya bar yang dag par rjes su mi mthong ba de dag byang chub nyid
21b5(sna tshogs): la gnas pa ste/ 'di ni gang yang dag par rjes su mi mthong / gang la'ang mngon par mi zhe na/ gang la'ang rnam par rtog par mi 'gyur te/ rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon
21b6(sna tshogs): pagang dag de ltar rnam par grol ba dang / rnam par grol bar sems mi skyed pa de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' yang dag pa zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon
21b7(sna tshogs): pagang dag sems can du 'du shes pa dang / byang chub tu 'du shes pa dang / byang chub kyi phyir sems bskyed na/ de dag ni byang chub las ring ste/ de ni byang chub dang nye ba
22a1(sna tshogs): ma yin no/ / rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ gang dag byang chub las ring ba 'am/ nye bar yang dag par rjes su mi mthong ba de dag byang chub dang
22a2(sna tshogs): ba ste/ de ni byang chub kyi phyir sems bskyed pa'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ ngas de la dgongs nas/ gang bdag gnyis su med par shes pa de ni/ sangs
22a3(sna tshogs): rgyas dang chos kyang rab tu shes so zhes bshad do/ / de ci'i phyir zhe na/ gnyis su med pa yongs su shes pas/ chos thams cad yongs su shes te/ de chos thams cad kyi/
22a4(sna tshogs): bdag gi ngo bo nyid sgom pa'i phyir ro// gang gnyis su med pa'i chos shes bya ba de ni/ sangs rgyas kyi chos shes pa ste/ chos gnyis su med par yongs su shes pas/ sangs
22a5(sna tshogs): rgyas kyi chos yongs su shes so/ / bdag yongs su shes pas/ khams gsum thams cad yongs su shes so// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ gang dag yongs su shes
22a6(sna tshogs): pa zhes bya ba de ni/ chos thams cad kyi pha rol lo// chos thams cad kyi pha rol yang gang zhe na/ gang pha rol nyid kyang mi dmigs/ pha rol tu rlom sems su mi byed/
22a7(sna tshogs): rol la mngon par mi zhen pa de ni/ yongs su shes pas pha rol tu song ba zhes bya ste/ ji skad du brjod pa bzhin du ni ma yin no// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/
22b1(sna tshogs): ltar 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i sa yin par rig par bya'o// gang la shes par bya ba dang / rtogs par bya ba phra rab tsam yang med pa de ni/ byang chub sems dpa'i shes rab kyi
22b2(sna tshogs): pha rol tu phyin pa ste/ de la ni 'ong ba 'am/ 'gro ba mi mngon no// gleng gzhi'i le'u zhes bya ste dang po'o// // bam po gnyis pa// / de
22b3(sna tshogs): nas bcom ldan 'das la/ tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bos 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das nga rgyal can mtshan ma la spyod pa rnams bstan pa 'di la skrag par 'gyur
22b4(sna tshogs): lags so/ / de nas tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bus/ tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo la 'di skad ces smras so// tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo/ 'di ni nga rgyal can rnams kyi yul
22b5(sna tshogs): ma yin/ rtogs pa ma yin pas/ de dag 'di la skrag par mi 'gyur ro// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ gang sdig pa'i grogs po'i lag tu song ba de dag ni 'di la skrag par gyur zin
22b6(sna tshogs): pas/ 'di ni de dag gi yul ma yin zhing ma rtogs so// tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo/ gang dag nga rgyal spong ba'i phyir zhugs shing / nga rgyal spong ba'i phyir brtson pa de dag ni
22b7(sna tshogs): 'di la skrag par 'gyur ro/ / de ci'i phyir zhe na/ nga rgyal yongs su shes pas/ nga rgyal med pa tshol zhing / nga rgyal spong ba tshol ba'i phyir ro// tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo
23a1(sna tshogs): gang dag nga rgyal mi dmigs shing / yang dag par mi mthong la/ rlom sems su mi byed cing / mngon par mi zhen pa de dag ni gang la'ang mi skrag/ gang
23a2(sna tshogs): la'ang mi dngang / gang la'ang dngang bar mi 'gyur ro// tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo/ nga rgyal can rnams kyi phyir chos bstan pa 'di zhus pa ma yin no// tshe dang ldan pa kun dga'
23a3(sna tshogs): bo'adi ni nga rgyal can rnams kyi yul ma yin te/ go skabs med do// gang dag nga rgyal spong ba'i phyir brtson zhing 'bad pa de dag ni/ yang dag par 'bad pa ma yin no//
23a4(sna tshogs): tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo/ nga rgyal zhes bya ba de ni/ lhag par byed pa sgro 'dogs pa'i tshig bla dgas so// gang dag nga rgyal la spyod cing lhag par byed pa sgro 'dogs par spyod
23a5(sna tshogs): pa de dag ni mtshungs par mi spyod do/ / mtshungs par spyod pa'ang chos 'di la the tsom za'o// tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo/ gang dag mnyam pa'ang mi dmigs/ mi mnyam pa'ang
23a6(sna tshogs): ma yin/ mnyam par yang rlom sems mi byed/ mi mnyam par yang ma yin/ mnyam par yang mngon par mi zhe na/ mi mnyam par yang ma yin pa de dag ni/ gang
23a7(sna tshogs): la'ang mi skrag/ mi dngang / dngang bar mi 'gyur ro// tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo/ 'di ni byis pa so so'i skye bo thams cad kyi yul ma yin te/ mi rtogs so//
23b1(sna tshogs): tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo/ 'di ni byis pa so so'i skye bo thams cad kyis shes shing rtogs pa ma yin no// tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo/ nyan thos kyi theg pa can rnams kyis
23b2(sna tshogs): kyang mi rtogs so/ / 'di ni gang rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa can chos zab mo la spyod pa de dag gis kyang mi rtogs so// tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo// byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa can
23b3(sna tshogs): gang dag mtshan ma la spyod pa/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis yongs su ma zin pa/ sdig pa'i grogs po'i lag tu song ba de dag kyang / chags pa med pa'i chos 'di dag mi rtogs
23b4(sna tshogs): shing yul ma yin te/ tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo// nyan thos kyi theg pa can bden pa mthong ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa can dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis bstan pa
23b5(sna tshogs): chos zab mo la mos pa/ gang chos 'di dag la 'thun par spyod pa dang / gang chos 'di khong du chud cing / spyod pa rnams ni ma gtogs/ kun dga' bo/ byang chub sems
23b6(sna tshogs): dpa' mtshan ma dang bral ba/ mtshan ma med pa la spyod pa/ sna tshogs med pa la spyod pa/ zab mo'i chos shin tu mthar phyin pa/ gang dag sems dang byang chub kyang mi dmigs
23b7(sna tshogs): shing chos gang yang tha dad du mi byed la/ yang dag par rjes su mi mthong ba de dag ni/ 'di lta bu'i chos la rmongs par mi 'gyur/ the tsom mi za'o// ci'i phyir zhe na/
24a1(sna tshogs): ngag chos thams cad dang rjes su 'thun par gnas te/ mi mthun par ni ma yin pa'i phyir ro// de dag gis gang dang gang la chos 'dri ba de dang des rjes su 'thun
24a2(sna tshogs): par lan 'debs shing / rjes su 'thun par smra bar byed do// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis/ tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// kun
24a3(sna tshogs): dga' bo ji ltar shA ri'i bu 'dis bshad pa de de bzhin te/ kun dga' bo chos bstan pa 'di dang / sangs rgyas kyi byang chub dang rjes su 'thun pa'i sangs rgyas kyi byang chub 'di ni
24a4(sna tshogs): nga rgyal can rnams kyi sa ma yin/ 'jug pa'i yul ma yin te/ kun dga' bo/ sangs rgyas kyi chos rgya chen po la ni dman pa la mos pa'i sems can rnams kyi sems mi
24a5(sna tshogs): 'jug go/ / kun dga' bo/ dman pa la mos pa nga rgyal can rnams ni nga rgyal gyi dbang gis 'gro bas/ de dag sangs rgyas kyi byang chub la mi mthun par gnas so// kun dga'
24a6(sna tshogs): boH'khor 'di ni gtsang ma ste/ sngon gyi rgyal ba rnams la bya ba byas shing / dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa/ sangs rgyas mang po la bsnyen bkur byas pa/ zab mo la mos pa/
24a7(sna tshogs): zab mo spyod pa ste/ kun dga' bo/ 'khor 'di la de bzhin gshegs pas yid bstan nas/ chos mngon par ston gyis/ rjes su srung po'i chos ni cung zad kyang mi sngon no//
24b1(sna tshogs): kun dga' bo/ 'khor 'di ni snying po ste/ sa zhag dang / gseg ma dang / b+ho mo med pa/ sangs rgyas brgya stong mang po la bsnyen bkur byas pa/ snying po la
24b2(sna tshogs): rab tu gnas pa'o/ / kun dga' bo/ gseg ma dang gyo mo zhes bya ba de ni byis pa so so'i skye bo rnams kyi tshig bla dgas te/ gang dag chos 'di la go skabs med pa'o//
24b3(sna tshogs): kun dga' bo/ sa zhag ces bya ba 'di ni/ sems can nga rgyal can rnams kyi tshig bla dgas so// kun dga' bo/ 'khor 'di ni nga rgyal med pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba chen
24b4(sna tshogs): pos mngon par 'phags pa'o/ / kun dga' bo/ 'di lta ste/ dper na klu'i rgyal po ma dros pa rab tu dga' bar gyur te/ dga' ba dang yid bde ba skyes nas/ rang gi
24b5(sna tshogs): gnas na 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga spyod cing / rang gi gnas na rab tu dga' bar yan lag brgyad dang ldan pa'i char pa'i chu chen po 'bebs so// de'i bur gyur pa de dag kyang rab tu
24b6(sna tshogs): dga' nas/ rang rang gi gnas na 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga 'byor cing ldan par gyur te/ rtse zhing char chen po 'bebs so// kun dga' bo de bzhin du/ de bzhin gshegs pa
24b7(sna tshogs): dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyang chos kyi char chen po 'bebs so/ / gang sras thu bo byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag kyang / 'jig rten
25a1(sna tshogs): gyi khams 'di nas rang rang gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing du song ste/ chos kun 'byung ba 'di la brtsams nas de bzhin gshegs pa de dag gi spyan sngar chos kyi
25a2(sna tshogs): char chen po gtong zhing / chos kyi char chen po rab tu 'bebs so// kun dga' bo/ 'di lta ste/ dper na klu'i rgyal po rgya mtsho ni/ gang gi tshe rab tu dga' bar gyur pa de'i tshe/
25a3(sna tshogs): rang gi gnas nas char gyi rgyun chen po 'bebs so// gang dag gnas de na gnas par gyur pa'i klu de dag gis kyang char gyi rgyun de mnos nas dga' bar gyur te/ char gyi rgyun des
25a4(sna tshogs): bde bar shes so/ / gang dag de'i bur gyur pa de dag kyang / char gyi rgyun de bzod cing / char gyi rgyun des mchog tu dga' ba thob bo// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ kun dga' bo/
25a5(sna tshogs): klu gzhan dag gis char gyi rgyun de mi bzod la/ klu gzhan dag ni char gyi rgyun nges bde bar mi shes shing / char gyi rgyun de dag gis dga' bar mi 'gyur ba'i phyir ro// kun dag
25a6(sna tshogs): bo de bzhin du/ gang dag de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos dkon mchog la lhag par chags pa dang / gang dag de bzhin gshegs pa'i sras thu bo byang chub sems dpa' sems
25a7(sna tshogs): dpa' chen po dge ba'i rtsa ba byas pa/ bsam pa rgya che ba/ chos zab mo'i tshul las nges par skyes pa de dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi tshul gyi char chen po 'di bas
25b1(sna tshogs): do/ / thos nas rab tu dga' zhing mgu ste bde bar shes so// kun dga' bo/ de bzhin gshegs pas don gyi dbang 'di la brten te/ bsam pa dag pa'i 'khor du seng ge'i
25b2(sna tshogs): sgra chen po sgrog cing / chos kyi char chen po 'bebs so// kun dga' bo/ 'di lta ste/ dper na 'khor lo sgyur ba'i rgyal po rin po che'i mdzod mang po bsam pa dang ldan pa
25b3(sna tshogs): des/ bu mang po rigs dang ldan zhing / rgyud kyis kyang dag pa de dag thams cad bkug nas rin po che'i mdzod bgos te/ bu gang la'ang mi bslu bar byin no// de ltar bgos
25b4(sna tshogs): pa de dag 'khor lo sgyur ba'i rgyal po de dga' ba dang mgu ba chen po lhag par skyes nas 'khor lo sgyur ba'i rgyal po dang don mtshungs par gyur to snyam ste/ bdag bde bar shes so//
25b5(sna tshogs): kun dga' bo de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi rgyal po/ chos kyi bdag po rang byung gis kyangango sras de dag bsdus nas/ chos rin po che'i mdzod 'di mnyam par bgos
25b6(sna tshogs): te/ sras de dag gang la'ang mi slu bas/ de dag gang la dga' ba dang / mgu ba dang / gus pa cher skyed cing / don mthun pa sangs rgyas kyi rigs mi gcod par
25b7(sna tshogs): gnas so/ / kun dga' bo/ sems can gzhan dman pa la mos pa/ nga rgyal can lta ba la spyod pa/ mtshan ma la spyod pa/ dmigs pa la spyod pa/ nga'o snyam
26a1(sna tshogs): pa'i nga rgyal gyis bcom pa/ 'dod chags dang / zhe sdang dang / gti mug gi zil gyis gnon pa/ log pa'i lam du dong ba rnams kyis chos rin
26a2(sna tshogs): po che 'di bzod par mi nus so/ / kun dga' bo/ dman pa la mos pa'i sems can rnams kyis 'khor lo sgyur ba'i nor ma 'dod kyi/ kun dga' bo/ gang dag 'khor lo
26a3(sna tshogs): sgyusbyar ba'i bur gyur pa de dag ni/ 'khor lo sgyur ba'i nor 'dod do// kun dga' bo/ sems can dbul po rnams ni 'khor lo rin po che dang / glang po rin po che dang /
26a4(sna tshogs): rin po che dang / nor bu rin po che dang / bud med rin po che dang / khyim bdag rin po che dang / blon po rin po che dang / gos mang po dang / gser dang / nor bu dang /
26a5(sna tshogs): mu tig dang / bai DUR+Ya dang / dung dang / man shel dang / b+hu ru dang / sa le sbram dang / dngul mang po dag bgos pa mi 'dzin te/ rnyed kyang dga' bar kun tu spyo
26a6(sna tshogs): par mi nus shing / rin thang chung ngur 'tshong la mi mkhas pas 'dor ro// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de dag rin po che la mi mkhas pa'i phyir ro// kun dga' bo/ sems can dngul
26a7(sna tshogs): po ni rin po che 'di'i ming ni 'di'o zhes bya bar rin po che rnams kyi ming yang mi shes so/ / kun dga' bo de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa'i sras bden pa mthong ba rnams dang
26b1(sna tshogs): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag ni/ chos rin po che'i mdzod 'di tshol ba ste/ chos rin po che dmigs su med pa/ stong pa nyid dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas
26b2(sna tshogs): kyi chos dang ldan pa 'di 'dod cing bzod de/ de dag nges bya ba byed do// sems can dbul po thos pa dang bral ba/ thos pa nyams pa/ mig dang mi ldan pa'i byis pa de
26b3(sna tshogs): ngag ni/ chos rin po che'i mdzod rnyed kyang ci zhig bya zhes 'dor zhing / gzhan la sbyin par sems so// kun dga' bo/ gdol pa dang / g.yung po dang / sgyu ma
26b4(sna tshogs): mkhan dang / dbul pos 'tsho ba'i sems can gang gzhan la las rin po che'i mdzod rnyed na bdag mi spyod de/ rin thang chung ngur 'tshong zhing 'dor ro// kun dga' bo//
26b5(sna tshogs): sems can dbul po zhes bya ba de ni mu stegs can thams cad dang / gang dag mu stegs can gyi nyan thos rnams kyi tshig bla dgas so// kun dga' bo/ sems can
26b6(sna tshogs): dbul po zhes bya ba de ni byis pa so so'i skye bo lta ba'i 'dam du bying ba/ dmigs pa can/ 'ching ba la mngon par zhen pa/ mtshan ma la spyod pa/ lam log par
26b7(sna tshogs): song ba rnams kyi tshig bla dgas te/ de dag ni chos rin po 'di rnyeng na kun tu spyod mi nus shing 'dor te/ don med par yang gzhan la'ang sbyin par byed de/ kun dga' bo
27a1(sna tshogs): gang sangs rgyas kyi sras/ sangs rgyas kyi spyod yul la spyod pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs rgyun mi 'chad par gnas pa de dag rin po che 'di la yongs
27a2(sna tshogs): spyod do/ / rnyed nas kyang chung mi gson cing / 'di la rin po cher 'du shes 'gyur ro// kun dga' bo/ was ni seng ge'i sgra sgrog mi nus so// kun dga' bo/ gang
27a3(sna tshogs): seng ge'i phrug gur gyur la/ seng ge chen pos bskyed pa de dag seng ge'i sgra sgrog go// kun dga' bo de bzhin du wa lta bu ni byis pa so so'i skye bo log par lta ba thams cad de
27a4(sna tshogs): de dag gis ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i seng ge'i sgra dang / yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas seng ge chen po'i chos yongs su longs spyod par mi nus so// kun dga' bo
27a5(sna tshogs): gang yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi sras sangs rgyas kyi seng ge chen po dang / rang byung gi ye shes kyis bskyed pa dag ni yang dag por rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi seng po
27a6(sna tshogs): sgra sgrog cing kun tu spyod do/ / de nas bcom ldan 'das la/ tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bus 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das 'di ltar de bzhin
27a7(sna tshogs): gshegs pa'i 'khor yongs su dag pa 'dus pa 'di ngo mtshar to/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor/ rang byung gi 'khor/ mi tshugs pa'i 'khor/

27b2(sna tshogs): 'das kyis/ tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// shA ri'i bu/ khyod 'khor 'di'i yon tan yongs su brjod dam/ gsol pa/ bcom
27b3(sna tshogs): ldan 'das bdag gis 'khor 'di'i yon tan yongs su brjod pa'i rngo mi thogs lags so/ / de ci'i slad du zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das 'khor 'di ni ri rab dang 'dra ste/ yon
27b4(sna tshogs): hatan mtha' yas pa dang ldan pa lags pa'i slad du'o/ / bka' stsal pa/ shA ra dA ti'i bu de de bzhin te/ 'khor 'di ni yon tan mtha' yas pa dang ldan pa ste/ 'khor
27b5(sna tshogs): 'di'i yon tan gyi mtha' yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyis kyang rtogs par mi nus na/ sems can gzhan thams cad kyis lha ci smos/ shA ra dwa ti'i bu
27b6(sna tshogs): de bzhin gshegs pas bslus pa ma yin zhing / 'di la de bzhin gshegs pas rtsol ba ci'ang mi mdzad de/ rang gi dge ba'i rtsa bas/ nga'i ming thos nas 'khor 'dir
27b7(sna tshogs): 'dus te/ de bzhin gshegs pas 'khor 'di ga la'ang ma glengs ma bsgos pa/ de dag rang gi dge ba'i rtsa bas bskul nas 'khor 'dir lhags so// 'di lta bu'i
28a1(sna tshogs): chos bstan pa la/ 'di lta bu'i sems can chen po 'du bar 'gyur ba ni de'i chos nyid do// shA ra dwa ti'i bu/ gang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das

28a3(sna tshogs): gyi dkyil 'khor gdon mi za bar 'byung ba ni chos bstan pa 'di'i chos nyid do/ / kun dga' bo'i le'u zhes bya ste gnyis pa'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das

28a5(sna tshogs): kyi pha rol tu phyin pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya ba la/ byang chub sems dpa'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa gang zhe na/ gang chos thams cad kyi tshu rol rtog
28a6(sna tshogs): pa ste/ do ni bstan par mi nus mod kyi/ ji ltar khyod shes par 'gyur ba dang / ji ltar shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa tha snyad kyi tshig tu 'gyur ba de ltar rab tu bshad par
